        function switchTab(id, el) { document.querySelectorAll('[id^="section-"]').forEach(d => { d.classList.remove('show-section'); d.classList.add('hide-section'); }); document.getElementById('section-'+id).classList.remove('hide-section'); document.getElementById('section-'+id).classList.add('show-section'); document.getElementById('pageTitle').innerText = el ? el.innerText.trim() : 'Yönetim'; if(el) { document.querySelectorAll('.nav-item').forEach(n => n.classList.remove('active')); el.classList.add('active'); }}
        function toggleCountrySelect() { const type = document.getElementById('annType').value; const div = document.getElementById('countrySelectDiv'); if(type === 'ulke') div.classList.remove('hidden'); else div.classList.add('hidden'); }
        window.onload = function() { 
            const select = document.getElementById('annCountry'); select.innerHTML = '<option value="">Ülke Seçiniz...</option>'; 
            ulkelerTamListe.sort((a,b) => a.isim.localeCompare(b.isim)); ulkelerTamListe.forEach(ulke => { const opt = document.createElement('option'); opt.value = ulke.code; opt.text = ulke.isim + " (" + ulke.code + ")"; select.add(opt); }); 
            loadDashboard(); loadUsers(); loadListings(); loadTravel(); loadAcademy(); loadLaw(); loadAnnouncements(); renderCharts(); loadBorders(); loadTransfer(); loadSOS(); loadWaze();
            // Yeni Modüller
            loadMarketPrices();
            loadCatalogs();
            loadCameras();
            populateAdminCountries(); // Admin'deki katalog ülke listesini doldur
            const chatSelect = document.getElementById('chatUlkeSelect');
            if(typeof lokasyonVeritabani !== 'undefined'){ Object.keys(lokasyonVeritabani).forEach(kod => { const opt = document.createElement('option'); opt.value = kod; opt.text = lokasyonVeritabani[kod].isim; chatSelect.add(opt); }); }
        };

        // --- DASHBOARD, USERS, LISTINGS ---
        async function loadDashboard() { const { count: u } = await sb.from('profiles').select('*', {count:'exact', head:true}); const { count: l } = await sb.from('ilanlar').select('*', {count:'exact', head:true}); const { count: p } = await sb.from('listings').select('*', {count:'exact', head:true}).eq('status','pending'); const { count: a } = await sb.from('announcements').select('*', {count:'exact', head:true}); document.getElementById('dashUsers').innerText = u || 0; document.getElementById('dashListings').innerText = l || 0; document.getElementById('dashPending').innerText = p || 0; document.getElementById('dashAnnounce').innerText = a || 0; }
        async function loadUsers() { const { data } = await sb.from('profiles').select('*').order('created_at', {ascending: false}); const tb = document.getElementById('usersTable'); tb.innerHTML = ''; if(!data || data.length === 0) { tb.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="4" class="text-center py-4">Kayıt yok.</td></tr>'; return; } data.forEach(user => { let statusColor = user.status === 'banned' ? 'text-red-400 bg-red-400/10' : 'text-emerald-400 bg-emerald-400/10'; tb.innerHTML += `<tr class="hover:bg-white/5 border-b border-slate-800"><td class="px-6 py-4 flex items-center gap-3"><div class="w-8 h-8 rounded-full bg-slate-700 flex items-center justify-center font-bold text-xs">${user.full_name?.substring(0,2)||'U'}</div><div><p>${user.full_name||'İsimsiz'}</p><p class="text-xs text-slate-500">${user.email}</p></div></td><td class="px-6 py-4">${user.role}</td><td class="px-6 py-4"><span class="px-2 py-1 rounded text-xs font-bold ${statusColor}">${user.status}</span></td><td class="px-6 py-4 text-right"><button onclick="sendMessageToUser('${user.id}', '${user.full_name}')" class="text-blue-400 mr-2"><i class="fa-solid fa-envelope"></i></button><button onclick="toggleBan('${user.id}', '${user.status}')" class="text-amber-400 mr-2"><i class="fa-solid fa-ban"></i></button><button onclick="delUser('${user.id}')" class="text-red-400"><i class="fa-solid fa-trash"></i></button></td></tr>`; }); }
        async function delUser(id) { if(confirm('Silinsin mi?')) { await sb.from('profiles').delete().eq('id', id); loadUsers(); } }
        async function toggleBan(id, st) { let newSt = st === 'active' ? 'banned' : 'active'; await sb.from('profiles').update({status: newSt}).eq('id', id); loadUsers(); }
        async function sendMessageToUser(uid, name) { const { value: txt } = await Swal.fire({ title: `Mesaj: ${name}`, input: 'text', inputPlaceholder: 'Mesajınız...' }); if(txt) { await sb.from('notifications').insert([{user_id: uid, title:'Yönetim', content:txt}]); Swal.fire('Gönderildi', '', 'success'); } }
        
        async function loadListings() { 
            const { data } = await sb.from('ilanlar').select('*').order('created_at', {ascending: false}); 
            const div = document.getElementById('listingsContainer'); 
            div.innerHTML = ''; 
            if(!data || data.length === 0) { 
                div.innerHTML = '<p class="text-center text-slate-500 py-10">Henüz hiç ilan yok.</p>'; 
                return; 
            } 
            data.forEach(l => { 
                let badge = l.status === 'active' ? '<span class="text-emerald-400 border border-emerald-400 px-2 rounded text-xs">Aktif</span>' : '<span class="text-amber-400 border border-amber-400 px-2 rounded text-xs">Bekliyor</span>'; 
                let icon = '<i class="fa-solid fa-file text-slate-500 text-2xl"></i>';
                if(l.category === 'Emlak') icon = '<i class="fa-solid fa-house text-emerald-400 text-2xl bg-emerald-400/10 p-2 rounded"></i>';
                if(l.category === 'İş İlanı') icon = '<i class="fa-solid fa-briefcase text-amber-400 text-2xl bg-amber-400/10 p-2 rounded"></i>';
                div.innerHTML += `
                <div class="bg-slate-800/50 p-4 rounded-xl flex justify-between items-center border border-white/5 hover:bg-slate-800 transition group">
                    <div class="flex items-center gap-4">
                        ${icon}
                        <div><h4 class="font-bold text-white">${l.title}</h4><p class="text-xs text-slate-400">${l.category} • ${l.price}</p></div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="flex items-center gap-3">
                        ${badge}
                        ${l.status !== 'active' ? `<button onclick="updateStatus('${l.id}','active')" class="text-emerald-400 hover:scale-110 transition"><i class="fa-solid fa-check"></i></button>` : ''}
                        <button onclick="delListing('${l.id}')" class="text-red-400 hover:text-red-500 hover:scale-110 transition bg-red-500/10 p-2 rounded"><i class="fa-solid fa-trash"></i></button>
                    </div>
                </div>`; 
            }); 
        }
        async function updateStatus(id, status) { await sb.from('ilanlar').update({status}).eq('id', id); loadListings(); }
        async function delListing(id) { if(confirm('Bu ilan silinsin mi?')) { await sb.from('ilanlar').delete().eq('id', id); loadListings(); } }
        async function deleteAllListings() {
            if(confirm('DİKKAT: Veritabanındaki TÜM ilanlar silinecek! Onaylıyor musun?')) {
                const { error } = await sb.from('ilanlar').delete().neq('id', 0); // Hepsini sil
                if(!error) { Swal.fire('Temizlendi', 'Tüm ilanlar silindi.', 'success'); loadListings(); }
            }
        }

        // --- YENİ EKLENEN MARKET & KAMERA FONKSİYONLARI ---
        
        // 1. Ülke Listesini Admin Dropdown'a Doldur
        function populateAdminCountries() {
            const select = document.getElementById('catCountry');
            if(!select) return;
            select.innerHTML = '<option value="">Ülke Seçiniz...</option>';
            marketUlkeListesi.sort((a,b) => a.isim.localeCompare(b.isim));
            marketUlkeListesi.forEach(ulke => {
                const opt = document.createElement('option');
                opt.value = ulke.code;
                opt.text = `${ulke.bayrak} ${ulke.isim}`;
                select.add(opt);
            });
        }

        async function updateCurrency() {
            document.getElementById('rateEuro').innerHTML = '<i class="fa-solid fa-spinner fa-spin"></i>';
            setTimeout(() => {
                document.getElementById('rateEuro').innerText = "36.80 ₺";
                document.getElementById('rateUsd').innerText = "34.10 ₺";
                document.getElementById('rateGold').innerText = "2485 ₺";
                Swal.fire({toast:true, position:'top-end', icon:'success', title:'Kurlar Güncellendi', timer:1500, showConfirmButton:false});
            }, 1000);
        }

        const temelUrunler = [
            {id:1, name: "Ayçiçek Yağı (1L)", aldi: 1.49, lidl: 1.49, tr: 1.80},
            {id:2, name: "Un (1kg)", aldi: 0.79, lidl: 0.79, tr: 0.90},
            {id:3, name: "Toz Şeker (1kg)", aldi: 1.29, lidl: 1.19, tr: 1.30},
            {id:4, name: "Dana Kıyma (500g)", aldi: 4.99, lidl: 4.89, tr: 6.50},
            {id:5, name: "Yumurta (10'lu)", aldi: 1.99, lidl: 1.99, tr: 2.20},
        ];

        function loadMarketPrices() {
            const tbody = document.getElementById('marketTable');
            tbody.innerHTML = '';
            temelUrunler.forEach(item => {
                const min = Math.min(item.aldi, item.lidl, item.tr);
                let winner = '';
                if(min === item.tr) winner = '<span class="text-red-400 font-bold"><i class="fa-solid fa-trophy"></i> TR Market</span>';
                else if(min === item.lidl) winner = '<span class="text-yellow-400 font-bold">Lidl</span>';
                else winner = '<span class="text-blue-400 font-bold">Aldi</span>';

                tbody.innerHTML += `<tr class="hover:bg-white/5 border-b border-slate-800"><td class="px-4 py-3 font-bold text-white">${item.name}</td><td class="px-4 py-3 text-center">${item.aldi}€</td><td class="px-4 py-3 text-center">${item.lidl}€</td><td class="px-4 py-3 text-center">${item.tr}€</td><td class="px-4 py-3 text-center text-xs">${winner}</td><td class="px-4 py-3 text-right"><button onclick="editPrice(${item.id})" class="bg-indigo-600 text-white px-2 py-1 rounded text-xs hover:bg-indigo-500">Düzenle</button></td></tr>`;
            });
        }

        async function fetchMarketPrices() {
            Swal.fire({title: 'Bot Çalışıyor...', text: 'Market siteleri taranıyor', didOpen: () => Swal.showLoading()});
            setTimeout(() => {
                temelUrunler.forEach(u => { u.aldi = (u.aldi + (Math.random() * 0.1 - 0.05)).toFixed(2); u.lidl = (u.lidl + (Math.random() * 0.1 - 0.05)).toFixed(2); });
                loadMarketPrices();
                Swal.fire('Tamamlandı', 'Fiyatlar güncellendi.', 'success');
            }, 2000);
        }

        async function editPrice(id) {
            const product = temelUrunler.find(p => p.id === id);
            const { value: formValues } = await Swal.fire({
                title: `${product.name} Fiyatı`,
                html: `<label>Aldi (€)</label><input id="swal-aldi" class="swal2-input" value="${product.aldi}"><label>Lidl (€)</label><input id="swal-lidl" class="swal2-input" value="${product.lidl}"><label>TR Market (€)</label><input id="swal-tr" class="swal2-input" value="${product.tr}">`,
                focusConfirm: false,
                preConfirm: () => [ document.getElementById('swal-aldi').value, document.getElementById('swal-lidl').value, document.getElementById('swal-tr').value ]
            });
            if (formValues) { product.aldi = parseFloat(formValues[0]); product.lidl = parseFloat(formValues[1]); product.tr = parseFloat(formValues[2]); loadMarketPrices(); Swal.fire('Kaydedildi', '', 'success'); }
        }

        async function saveCatalog() {
            const country = document.getElementById('catCountry').value;
            const market = document.getElementById('catMarket').value;
            const link = document.getElementById('catLink').value;
            const image = document.getElementById('catImage').value;
            if(!link) return Swal.fire('Hata', 'Link gerekli', 'error');
            await sb.from('catalogs').insert([{ country, market, link, image_url: image, active: true }]);
            Swal.fire('Eklendi', '', 'success');
            loadCatalogs();
        }

        async function loadCatalogs() {
            const div = document.getElementById('catalogList');
            div.innerHTML = '<p class="text-xs text-slate-500">Yükleniyor...</p>';
            const { data } = await sb.from('catalogs').select('*').order('created_at', {ascending: false});
            div.innerHTML = '';
            if(!data || data.length===0) div.innerHTML = '<p class="text-xs text-slate-500">Katalog yok.</p>';
            else {
                data.forEach(c => {
                    const ulke = marketUlkeListesi.find(u => u.code === c.country);
                    const bayrak = ulke ? ulke.bayrak : '';
                    div.innerHTML += `<div class="flex items-center justify-between bg-slate-800 p-2 rounded border border-slate-700"><div class="flex items-center gap-3"><img src="${c.image_url || 'https://via.placeholder.com/40'}" class="w-8 h-10 object-cover rounded"><div><p class="text-xs font-bold text-white">${c.market}</p><p class="text-[10px] text-slate-400">${bayrak} ${c.country}</p></div></div><button onclick="delCatalog('${c.id}')" class="text-red-400 hover:text-white"><i class="fa-solid fa-trash"></i></button></div>`;
                });
            }
        }
        async function delCatalog(id) { if(confirm('Silinsin mi?')) { await sb.from('catalogs').delete().eq('id', id); loadCatalogs(); } }

        async function loadCameras() {
            const tbody = document.getElementById('cameraList');
            tbody.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="4" class="p-4 text-center text-xs text-slate-500">Yükleniyor...</td></tr>';
            const { data } = await sb.from('border_cameras').select('*');
            tbody.innerHTML = '';
            if(!data || data.length===0) tbody.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="4" class="p-4 text-center text-xs text-slate-500">Kamera yok.</td></tr>';
            else {
                data.forEach(c => {
                    tbody.innerHTML += `<tr class="hover:bg-white/5 border-b border-slate-800"><td class="px-4 py-3 font-bold text-white">${c.name}</td><td class="px-4 py-3"><span class="bg-slate-700 px-2 py-1 rounded text-[10px]">${c.country}</span></td><td class="px-4 py-3 text-xs font-mono text-slate-400 truncate max-w-[200px]">${c.stream_url}</td><td class="px-4 py-3 text-right"><button onclick="delCamera('${c.id}')" class="text-red-400 hover:text-white"><i class="fa-solid fa-trash"></i></button></td></tr>`;
                });
            }
        }

        async function addCamera() {
            const { value: formValues } = await Swal.fire({
                title: 'Yeni Kamera',
                html: `<input id="cam-name" class="swal2-input" placeholder="Kapı Adı (Örn: Kapıkule)"><input id="cam-country" class="swal2-input" placeholder="Ülke (Örn: TR)"><input id="cam-url" class="swal2-input" placeholder="Yayın Linki (m3u8/Youtube)">`,
                focusConfirm: false,
                preConfirm: () => [document.getElementById('cam-name').value, document.getElementById('cam-country').value, document.getElementById('cam-url').value]
            });
            if (formValues) {
                await sb.from('border_cameras').insert([{ name: formValues[0], country: formValues[1], stream_url: formValues[2] }]);
                Swal.fire('Eklendi', '', 'success');
                loadCameras();
            }
        }
        async function delCamera(id) { if(confirm('Silinsin mi?')) { await sb.from('border_cameras').delete().eq('id', id); loadCameras(); } }

        // --- ADZUNA API ENTEGRASYONU ---
        async function fetchAdzunaJobs() {
            const btn = document.getElementById('btnAdzuna');
            const logBox = document.getElementById('jobLog');
            const country = document.getElementById('adzunaCountry').value;
            const query = document.getElementById('adzunaQuery').value;
            
            if(!query) return Swal.fire('Hata', 'Lütfen aranacak meslek girin.', 'warning');

            btn.disabled = true; btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fa-solid fa-spinner fa-spin"></i> Aranıyor...';
            logBox.classList.remove('hidden'); logBox.innerHTML = `> ${country.toUpperCase()} ülkesinde '${query}' aranıyor...\n`;

            try {
                const url = `https://api.adzuna.com/v1/api/jobs/${country}/search/1?app_id=${ADZUNA_ID}&app_key=${ADZUNA_KEY}&results_per_page=20&what=${encodeURIComponent(query)}`;
                const response = await fetch(url);
                const data = await response.json();
                
                let count = 0;
                
                if(data.results && data.results.length > 0) {
                    for (const job of data.results) {
                        const title = job.title.replace(/<\/?[^>]+(>|$)/g, ""); 
                        const company = job.company.display_name;
                        const location = job.location.display_name;
                        const desc = job.description.replace(/<\/?[^>]+(>|$)/g, "").substring(0, 300) + '...';
                        const url = job.redirect_url;
                        const salary = job.salary_min ? `€${Math.round(job.salary_min)}` : 'Görüşülür';
                        const logoUrl = `https://ui-avatars.com/api/?name=${encodeURIComponent(company)}&background=random&color=fff`;

                        const { error } = await sb.from('ilanlar').insert([{
                            title: `${title} (${company})`,
                            price: salary,
                            category: 'İş İlanı',
                            sub_category: 'Tam Zamanlı',
                            status: 'active',
                            description: desc + `\n\nBaşvuru: ${url}`,
                            city: `${location} (${country.toUpperCase()})`,
                            image: logoUrl
                        }]);

                        if (!error) {
                            count++;
                            logBox.innerHTML += `> Eklendi: ${title}\n`;
                            logBox.scrollTop = logBox.scrollHeight;
                        }
                    }
                    Swal.fire('Başarılı', `${count} ilan eklendi!`, 'success');
                    loadListings();
                } else {
                    logBox.innerHTML += `> HATA: Sonuç bulunamadı.\n`;
                }
            } catch (err) {
                console.error(err);
                logBox.innerHTML += `> HATA: ${err.message}\n`;
            }
            btn.disabled = false; btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fa-solid fa-search"></i> GETİR';
        }

        // --- CAREERJET XML GENERATOR ---
        async function downloadCareerjetXML() {
            const { data, error } = await sb.from('ilanlar').select('*').eq('category', 'İş İlanı');

            if (error || !data || data.length === 0) {
                Swal.fire('Uyarı', 'İndirilecek iş ilanı bulunamadı.', 'warning');
                return;
            }

            let xmlContent = '<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8" ?>\n<jobs>\n';

            data.forEach(job => {
                let desc = job.description || "Detaylar için web sitemizi ziyaret edin.";
                desc = desc.replace(/&/g, '&').replace(/</g, '<').replace(/>/g, '>');
                
                // Buradaki domaini kendi domaininle değiştir
                let jobUrl = `https://www.platformavrupa.com/ilan_detay.html?id=${job.id}`;

                xmlContent += `  <job>\n`;
                xmlContent += `    <title><![CDATA[${job.title}]]></title>\n`;
                xmlContent += `    <url><![CDATA[${jobUrl}]]></url>\n`;
                xmlContent += `    <description><![CDATA[${desc}]]></description>\n`;
                xmlContent += `    <location><![CDATA[${job.city || 'Europe'}]]></location>\n`;
                xmlContent += `    <company><![CDATA[${job.sub_category || 'PlatformAvrupa'}]]></company>\n`; 
                xmlContent += `    <salary><![CDATA[${job.price || ''}]]></salary>\n`;
                xmlContent += `    <date><![CDATA[${new Date(job.created_at).toISOString().split('T')[0]}]]></date>\n`;
                xmlContent += `    <referencenumber><![CDATA[${job.id}]]></referencenumber>\n`;
                xmlContent += `  </job>\n`;
            });

            xmlContent += '</jobs>';

            const blob = new Blob([xmlContent], { type: 'text/xml' });
            const url = window.URL.createObjectURL(blob);
            const a = document.createElement('a');
            a.href = url;
            a.download = 'jobs.xml';
            document.body.appendChild(a);
            a.click();
            window.URL.revokeObjectURL(url);

            Swal.fire('Başarılı', 'jobs.xml indirildi. Bunu Careerjet\'e gönderebilirsin.', 'success');
        }

        // --- EMLAK SİMÜLATÖRÜ ---
        async function generateEuData() {
            const city = document.getElementById('botCity').value;
            const btn = document.getElementById('btnFetchEstate');
            const logBox = document.getElementById('estateLog');

            btn.disabled = true; btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fa-solid fa-spinner fa-spin"></i> İlanlar Oluşturuluyor...';
            logBox.classList.remove('hidden'); logBox.innerHTML = `> ${city} için veri üretiliyor...\n`;

            const images = ['https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1560448204-e02f11c3d0e2?w=500', 'https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1572120360610-d971b9d7767c?w=500', 'https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1512917774080-9991f1c4c750?w=500'];
            let count = 0;
            for(let i=0; i<5; i++) {
                const randPrice = Math.floor(Math.random() * 2000) + 600;
                const randImg = images[i % 3] + `&r=${Math.random()}`;
                const { error } = await sb.from('ilanlar').insert([{ title: `Kiralık Daire - ${city} Merkez`, price: `€${randPrice}`, category: 'Emlak', sub_category: 'Kiralık', status: 'active', description: `${city} merkezinde, toplu taşımaya yakın, full eşyalı harika daire.`, image: randImg, city: city }]);
                if (!error) { count++; logBox.innerHTML += `> Eklendi: Daire (€${randPrice})\n`; logBox.scrollTop = logBox.scrollHeight; }
            }
            btn.disabled = false; btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fa-solid fa-bolt mr-2"></i> Üret';
            Swal.fire('Harika!', `${count} adet Avrupa ilanı başarıyla oluşturuldu.`, 'success');
            loadListings();
        }

        // --- DİĞER MODÜLLER ---
        function initChatModule() { sb.channel('admin-chat').on('postgres_changes', { event: '*', schema: 'public', table: 'messages' }, payload => { if(payload.eventType === 'INSERT') renderMsg(payload.new); else if(payload.eventType === 'DELETE') document.getElementById(`msg-${payload.old.id}`)?.remove(); }).subscribe(); loadChatMessages(); }
        async function loadChatMessages() { const { data } = await sb.from('messages').select('*').order('created_at', {ascending: false}).limit(50); document.getElementById('chatMonitorBox').innerHTML = ''; data?.forEach(renderMsg); }
        function renderMsg(m) { const div = document.getElementById('chatMonitorBox'); let adminClass = (m.user_name === 'Platform Yönetimi') ? 'chat-admin-msg' : 'border-l-2 border-slate-600'; const html = `<div id="msg-${m.id}" class="bg-slate-800/50 p-3 rounded mb-2 text-sm group relative ${adminClass}"><div class="flex justify-between text-xs text-slate-400 mb-1"><span class="font-bold ${m.user_name === 'Platform Yönetimi' ? 'text-red-400' : 'text-slate-300'}">${m.room_id} • ${m.user_name}</span><button onclick="delMsg('${m.id}')" class="text-red-400 hidden group-hover:block hover:bg-white/10 p-1 rounded"><i class="fa-solid fa-trash"></i></button></div><p class="text-slate-200">${m.content}</p></div>`; div.insertAdjacentHTML('afterbegin', html); }
        async function delMsg(id) { if(confirm('Mesaj silinsin mi?')) await sb.from('messages').delete().eq('id', id); }
        async function adminMesajGonder(e) { e.preventDefault(); const content = document.getElementById('chatMsgInput').value.trim(); const sender = document.getElementById('fakeSenderName').value.trim() || 'Admin'; let room = 'genel'; const ulke = document.getElementById('chatUlkeSelect').value; if(ulke !== 'genel') { const sehir = document.getElementById('chatSehirSelect').value; if(!sehir) { Swal.fire('Hata','Şehir seçmelisiniz','error'); return; } room = sehir; } if(!content) return; await sb.from('messages').insert([{room_id: room, user_name: sender, content}]); document.getElementById('chatMsgInput').value = ''; Swal.fire({toast:true, position:'top-end', icon:'success', title:'Mesaj Gönderildi', showConfirmButton:false, timer:1500}); }
        function chatUlkeDegisti() { const k = document.getElementById('chatUlkeSelect').value; const s = document.getElementById('chatSehirSelect'); s.innerHTML = ''; if(k === 'genel') { s.disabled = true; s.classList.add('opacity-50', 'cursor-not-allowed'); s.innerHTML='<option>Genel Sohbet</option>'; } else { s.disabled = false; s.classList.remove('opacity-50', 'cursor-not-allowed'); if(typeof lokasyonVeritabani !== 'undefined' && lokasyonVeritabani[k]) { lokasyonVeritabani[k].sehirler.sort().forEach(c => { const o = document.createElement('option'); o.value = c; o.text = c; s.add(o); }); } } }
        const fakeNames = ["Ahmet Yılmaz", "Canan Dağ", "Mehmet Öztürk", "Elif Kaya", "Ali Vural"];
        function generateRandomName() { document.getElementById('fakeSenderName').value = fakeNames[Math.floor(Math.random() * fakeNames.length)]; }
        function setAdminName() { document.getElementById('fakeSenderName').value = "Platform Yönetimi"; }
        async function publishAnnouncement() { const btn = document.getElementById('pubBtn'); const title = document.getElementById('annTitle').value; const content = document.getElementById('annContent').value; const type = document.getElementById('annType').value; const country = document.getElementById('annCountry').value; const file = document.getElementById('annImage').files[0]; if(!title) return Swal.fire('Hata', 'Başlık gerekli', 'error'); btn.innerHTML = 'Yükleniyor...'; btn.disabled = true; let imgUrl = null; if(file) { const name = `news_${Date.now()}_${file.name}`; try { await sb.storage.from('images').upload(name, file); const { data } = sb.storage.from('images').getPublicUrl(name); imgUrl = data.publicUrl; } catch(e) {} } const countryCode = type === 'ulke' ? country : null; await sb.from('announcements').insert([{ title, content, image_url: imgUrl, type, country_code: countryCode }]); btn.innerHTML = 'Yayına Al'; btn.disabled = false; document.getElementById('annTitle').value = ''; document.getElementById('annContent').value = ''; loadAnnouncements(); Swal.fire('Başarılı', 'Yayınlandı', 'success'); }
        async function loadAnnouncements() { const { data } = await sb.from('announcements').select('*').order('created_at', {ascending: false}); const div = document.getElementById('activeAnnouncements'); div.innerHTML = ''; if(!data) return; data.forEach(a => { let img = a.image_url ? `<img src="${a.image_url}" loading="lazy" alt="${a.title}" class="w-12 h-12 rounded-lg object-cover">` : '<div class="w-12 h-12 bg-slate-700 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center text-slate-500"><i class="fa-solid fa-image"></i></div>'; let badge = a.type === 'ulke' ? `<span class="bg-red-500/20 text-red-400 px-2 py-1 rounded text-xs font-bold border border-red-500/30">${a.country_code} ÖZEL</span>` : `<span class="bg-blue-500/20 text-blue-400 px-2 py-1 rounded text-xs font-bold border border-blue-500/30">GENEL</span>`; div.innerHTML += `<div class="glass-panel p-4 rounded-xl flex justify-between items-center border border-white/5 hover:border-white/10 transition"><div class="flex gap-4 items-center">${img} <div><h4 class="font-bold text-white text-sm">${a.title}</h4><div class="flex gap-2 mt-1">${badge} <span class="text-xs text-slate-500">${new Date(a.created_at).toLocaleDateString()}</span></div></div></div><button onclick="delAnn('${a.id}')" class="w-8 h-8 rounded-full bg-red-500/10 text-red-400 hover:bg-red-500 hover:text-white transition flex items-center justify-center"><i class="fa-solid fa-trash text-xs"></i></button></div>`; }); }
        async function delAnn(id) { if(confirm('Silinsin mi?')) { await sb.from('announcements').delete().eq('id', id); loadAnnouncements(); } }
        function renderCharts() { new Chart(document.getElementById('trafficChart').getContext('2d'), { type: 'line', data: { labels: ['Pzt', 'Sal', 'Çar', 'Per', 'Cum'], datasets: [{ label: 'Ziyaretçi', data: [120, 190, 300, 500, 240], borderColor: '#4f46e5', backgroundColor: 'rgba(79, 70, 229, 0.1)', fill: true, tension: 0.4 }] }, options: { responsive: true, maintainAspectRatio: false, plugins: { legend: { display: false } }, scales: { y: { grid: { color: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)' } }, x: { grid: { display: false } } } } }); new Chart(document.getElementById('categoryChart').getContext('2d'), { type: 'doughnut', data: { labels: ['Emlak', 'Vasıta', 'İş'], datasets: [{ data: [30, 50, 20], backgroundColor: ['#4f46e5', '#10b981', '#f59e0b'], borderWidth: 0 }] }, options: { responsive: true, maintainAspectRatio: false, plugins: { legend: { position: 'bottom', labels: { color: 'white' } } } } }); }
        async function downloadSitemap() { const { data: listings } = await sb.from('listings').select('id, created_at').eq('status', 'active'); const { data: travels } = await sb.from('travel_packages').select('id, created_at'); let xmlContent = `<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>\n<urlset xmlns="http://www.sitemaps.org/schemas/sitemap/0.9">\n   <url>\n      <loc>https://www.platformavrupa.com/</loc>\n      <changefreq>daily</changefreq>\n      <priority>1.0</priority>\n   </url>`; listings?.forEach(item => { xmlContent += `\n   <url>\n      <loc>https://www.platformavrupa.com/ilan-detay.html?id=${item.id}</loc>\n      <lastmod>${item.created_at.split('T')[0]}</lastmod>\n      <changefreq>weekly</changefreq>\n      <priority>0.8</priority>\n   </url>`; }); travels?.forEach(item => { xmlContent += `\n   <url>\n      <loc>https://www.platformavrupa.com/seyahat-detay.html?id=${item.id}</loc>\n      <lastmod>${item.created_at.split('T')[0]}</lastmod>\n      <changefreq>weekly</changefreq>\n      <priority>0.8</priority>\n   </url>`; }); xmlContent += `\n</urlset>`; const blob = new Blob([xmlContent], { type: 'text/xml' }); const url = window.URL.createObjectURL(blob); const a = document.createElement('a'); a.href = url; a.download = 'sitemap.xml'; document.body.appendChild(a); a.click(); window.URL.revokeObjectURL(url); Swal.fire('Başarılı', 'sitemap.xml indirildi. Bunu hosting paneline yükle!', 'success'); }
        async function saveAcademy() { const title = document.getElementById('acadTitle').value; const url = document.getElementById('acadUrl').value; const category = document.getElementById('acadCategory').value || 'Genel'; const order = document.getElementById('acadOrder').value || 0; const desc = document.getElementById('acadDesc').value; if(!title || !url) return Swal.fire('Hata', 'Başlık ve Link gerekli', 'error'); await sb.from('academy_contents').insert([{ title, url, category, order_id: parseInt(order), description: desc }]); Swal.fire('Başarılı', 'Video eklendi', 'success'); document.getElementById('acadTitle').value = ''; document.getElementById('acadUrl').value = ''; document.getElementById('acadDesc').value = ''; loadAcademy(); }
        async function loadAcademy() { const { data } = await sb.from('academy_contents').select('*').order('order_id', {ascending: true}); const div = document.getElementById('academyList'); div.innerHTML = ''; if(!data || data.length === 0) { div.innerHTML = '<p class="text-center text-slate-500">Video yok.</p>'; return; } const grouped = {}; data.forEach(item => { if(!grouped[item.category]) grouped[item.category] = []; grouped[item.category].push(item); }); const getYoutubeId = (url) => { const match = url.match(/^.*(youtu.be\/|v\/|u\/\w\/|embed\/|watch\?v=|&v=)([^#&?]*).*/); return (match && match[2].length === 11) ? match[2] : null; }; Object.keys(grouped).forEach(cat => { let html = `<div class="mb-8"><h4 class="font-bold text-xl text-indigo-400 mb-4 border-b border-white/10 pb-2">${cat}</h4><div class="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-6">`; grouped[cat].forEach(vid => { const yId = getYoutubeId(vid.url); const thumb = yId ? `https://img.youtube.com/vi/${yId}/0.jpg` : 'https://via.placeholder.com/300x200?text=No+Image'; html += `<div class="glass-panel rounded-xl overflow-hidden group relative"><div class="relative h-40"><img src="${thumb}" loading="lazy" alt="${vid.title}" class="w-full h-full object-cover"><div class="absolute inset-0 bg-black/50 flex items-center justify-center opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition"><a href="${vid.url}" target="_blank" class="text-white text-3xl"><i class="fa-solid fa-play-circle"></i></a></div></div><div class="p-4"><div class="flex justify-between items-start mb-2"><h5 class="font-bold text-white line-clamp-1">${vid.title}</h5><span class="text-xs bg-slate-700 px-2 py-1 rounded text-slate-300">#${vid.order_id}</span></div><p class="text-xs text-slate-400 line-clamp-2 mb-3">${vid.description || 'Açıklama yok.'}</p><button onclick="delAcademy('${vid.id}')" class="w-full bg-red-500/10 hover:bg-red-500 text-red-400 hover:text-white py-2 rounded text-xs font-bold transition">Sil</button></div></div>`; }); html += `</div></div>`; div.innerHTML += html; }); }
        async function delAcademy(id) { if(confirm('Silinsin mi?')) { await sb.from('academy_contents').delete().eq('id', id); loadAcademy(); } }
        async function addLaw() { const { value: title } = await Swal.fire({ title: 'Yeni Makale', input: 'text' }); if(title) { await sb.from('law_articles').insert([{ title }]); loadLaw(); } }
        async function loadLaw() { const { data } = await sb.from('law_articles').select('*'); const ul = document.getElementById('lawList'); ul.innerHTML = ''; data?.forEach(l => ul.innerHTML += `<li class="flex justify-between p-2 hover:bg-white/5 rounded"><span>${l.title}</span><button onclick="delLaw('${l.id}')" class="text-red-400"><i class="fa-solid fa-trash"></i></button></li>`); }
        async function delLaw(id) { await sb.from('law_articles').delete().eq('id', id); loadLaw(); }

        // --- SINIR KAPILARI (FAIL-SAFE) ---
        async function loadBorders() {
            const div = document.getElementById('bordersContainer');
            const log = document.getElementById('borderLog');
            div.innerHTML = '<div class="col-span-3 text-center text-slate-500"><i class="fa-solid fa-spinner fa-spin text-2xl"></i><br>Veriler Hazırlanıyor...</div>';
            const { data, error } = await sb.from('borders').select('*').order('id');
            if(error) return div.innerHTML = '<div class="col-span-3 text-red-400">Veritabanı Hatası</div>';
            div.innerHTML = ''; 
            data.forEach(gate => {
                const html = `<div id="card-${gate.id}" class="glass-panel p-5 rounded-2xl border border-slate-700 relative group overflow-hidden"><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-3 opacity-10"><i class="fa-solid fa-road-barrier text-6xl"></i></div><div class="relative z-10"><div class="flex justify-between items-center mb-4"><h4 class="font-bold text-xl text-white">${gate.name}</h4><span class="text-xs bg-slate-700 px-2 py-1 rounded text-slate-300">ID: ${gate.id}</span></div><div class="space-y-3"><div class="bg-slate-800/50 p-3 rounded-lg border border-white/5"><p class="text-[10px] text-slate-500 uppercase font-bold mb-1 tracking-wider"><i class="fa-brands fa-google mr-1"></i>Google Trafik Verisi</p><p id="google-time-${gate.id}" class="font-bold text-lg text-slate-400 flex items-center gap-2"><i class="fa-solid fa-clock"></i> <span class="animate-pulse">Hesaplanıyor...</span></p></div><div class="bg-slate-800/50 p-3 rounded-lg border border-white/5"><p class="text-[10px] text-slate-500 uppercase font-bold mb-1 tracking-wider"><i class="fa-solid fa-building-columns mr-1"></i>Bakanlık Verisi</p><p class="font-bold text-white flex items-center gap-2"><i class="fa-solid fa-car"></i> ${gate.vehicle_count} Araç</p></div></div><div class="mt-4 pt-4 border-t border-white/5 text-[10px] text-slate-500 flex justify-between"><span>Canlı Veri</span><a href="https://www.google.com/maps/dir/${gate.origin_lat},${gate.origin_lng}/${gate.dest_lat},${gate.dest_lng}" target="_blank" class="text-indigo-400 hover:text-indigo-300">Haritada Bak <i class="fa-solid fa-arrow-up-right-from-square ml-1"></i></a></div></div></div>`;
                div.innerHTML += html;
            });
            try {
                const service = new google.maps.DistanceMatrixService();
                data.forEach(gate => {
                    const origin = new google.maps.LatLng(gate.origin_lat, gate.origin_lng);
                    const dest = new google.maps.LatLng(gate.dest_lat, gate.dest_lng);
                    service.getDistanceMatrix({ origins: [origin], destinations: [dest], travelMode: 'DRIVING', drivingOptions: { departureTime: new Date(), trafficModel: 'bestguess' } }, (response, status) => {
                        const timeEl = document.getElementById(`google-time-${gate.id}`);
                        const cardEl = document.getElementById(`card-${gate.id}`);
                        if (status === 'OK' && response.rows[0].elements[0].status === 'OK') {
                            const info = response.rows[0].elements[0];
                            const duration = info.duration_in_traffic || info.duration;
                            const mins = duration.value / 60;
                            let colorClass = "text-emerald-400";
                            if(mins > 120) { colorClass = "text-red-400"; cardEl.style.borderColor = "rgba(239, 68, 68, 0.5)"; }
                            else if(mins > 30) { colorClass = "text-amber-400"; cardEl.style.borderColor = "rgba(245, 158, 11, 0.5)"; }
                            else { cardEl.style.borderColor = "rgba(16, 185, 129, 0.5)"; }
                            timeEl.className = `font-bold text-lg ${colorClass} flex items-center gap-2`;
                            timeEl.innerHTML = `<i class="fa-solid fa-clock"></i> ${duration.text}`;
                            log.innerHTML += `\n> ${gate.name}: OK (${duration.text})`;
                        } else { timeEl.innerHTML = `<i class="fa-solid fa-triangle-exclamation"></i> Veri Yok`; log.innerHTML += `\n> ${gate.name}: HATA (${status})`; }
                    });
                });
            } catch (e) { log.innerHTML += `\n> Google API Hatası: ${e.message}`; }
        }

        // --- TRANSFER (Yolculuk & Kargo) ---
        async function loadTransfer() {
            const tripsDiv = document.getElementById('tripsList');
            const shipmentsDiv = document.getElementById('shipmentsList');
            tripsDiv.innerHTML = '<p class="text-slate-500 text-xs">Yükleniyor...</p>';
            shipmentsDiv.innerHTML = '<p class="text-slate-500 text-xs">Yükleniyor...</p>';
            const { data: trips } = await sb.from('trips').select('*').order('created_at', {ascending: false});
            tripsDiv.innerHTML = '';
            if(!trips || trips.length === 0) tripsDiv.innerHTML = '<p class="text-slate-500 text-sm">İlan yok.</p>';
            else {
                trips.forEach(t => {
                    const cargoBadge = t.is_cargo_allowed ? '<span class="text-green-400 ml-2 text-[10px] border border-green-500/30 px-1 rounded"><i class="fa-solid fa-box"></i> Kargo Alır</span>' : '';
                    tripsDiv.innerHTML += `<div class="bg-slate-800/50 p-4 rounded-xl border border-white/5 hover:border-blue-500/50 transition relative group"><div class="flex justify-between items-start mb-2"><div class="flex items-center gap-3"><div class="w-8 h-8 rounded-full bg-blue-600 flex items-center justify-center font-bold text-xs">${t.driver_name.substring(0,2)}</div><div><h5 class="font-bold text-white text-sm">${t.driver_name}</h5><p class="text-[10px] text-slate-400">${t.travel_date}</p></div></div><span class="font-bold text-lg text-emerald-400">${t.price}€</span></div><div class="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-slate-300 font-bold mb-2"><span>${t.from_city}</span> <i class="fa-solid fa-arrow-right text-slate-500 text-xs"></i> <span>${t.to_city}</span></div><div class="flex items-center gap-2 text-xs text-slate-500"><span><i class="fa-solid fa-chair"></i> ${t.seats_available} Boş</span>${cargoBadge}</div><button onclick="delTrip('${t.id}')" class="absolute top-2 right-2 text-red-400 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition hover:bg-white/10 p-1 rounded"><i class="fa-solid fa-trash"></i></button></div>`;
                });
            }
            const { data: ships } = await sb.from('shipments').select('*').order('created_at', {ascending: false});
            shipmentsDiv.innerHTML = '';
            if(!ships || ships.length === 0) shipmentsDiv.innerHTML = '<p class="text-slate-500 text-sm">Talep yok.</p>';
            else {
                ships.forEach(s => {
                    shipmentsDiv.innerHTML += `<div class="bg-slate-800/50 p-4 rounded-xl border border-white/5 hover:border-amber-500/50 transition relative group"><div class="flex justify-between items-start mb-2"><h5 class="font-bold text-white text-sm"><i class="fa-solid fa-box text-amber-400 mr-1"></i> ${s.description}</h5><span class="text-[10px] bg-slate-700 px-2 py-1 rounded text-slate-300">${s.status}</span></div><div class="flex items-center gap-2 text-xs text-slate-300 mb-1"><span>${s.from_city}</span> <i class="fa-solid fa-arrow-right text-slate-500 text-[10px]"></i> <span>${s.to_city}</span></div><p class="text-[10px] text-slate-500">Gönderen: ${s.sender_name}</p><button onclick="delShipment('${s.id}')" class="absolute top-2 right-2 text-red-400 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition hover:bg-white/10 p-1 rounded"><i class="fa-solid fa-trash"></i></button></div>`;
                });
            }
        }
        async function delTrip(id) { if(confirm('Silinsin mi?')) { await sb.from('trips').delete().eq('id', id); loadTransfer(); } }
        async function delShipment(id) { if(confirm('Silinsin mi?')) { await sb.from('shipments').delete().eq('id', id); loadTransfer(); } }

        // --- YOL YARDIM & SOS MODÜLÜ ---
        async function loadSOS() {
            const sosList = document.getElementById('sosList');
            const servicesTable = document.getElementById('servicesTable');
            sosList.innerHTML = '<p class="text-slate-500 text-xs">Yükleniyor...</p>';
            const { data: alerts } = await sb.from('sos_alerts').select('*').order('created_at', {ascending: false});
            sosList.innerHTML = '';
            if(!alerts || alerts.length === 0) sosList.innerHTML = '<div class="text-center py-4 bg-slate-800/30 rounded-lg"><i class="fa-solid fa-check-circle text-green-500 mb-2"></i><p class="text-xs text-slate-400">Aktif yardım çağrısı yok.</p></div>';
            else {
                alerts.forEach(a => {
                    sosList.innerHTML += `<div class="bg-red-900/10 border border-red-500/30 p-4 rounded-xl relative pulse-red"><div class="flex justify-between items-start mb-2"><h5 class="font-bold text-white text-sm"><i class="fa-solid fa-triangle-exclamation text-red-500 mr-2"></i>${a.issue_type}</h5><span class="text-[10px] text-slate-400">${new Date(a.created_at).toLocaleTimeString()}</span></div><p class="text-sm text-slate-200 mb-1 font-bold">${a.user_name}</p><p class="text-xs text-slate-400 mb-2"><i class="fa-solid fa-location-dot mr-1"></i> ${a.location_text}</p><div class="flex gap-2"><a href="tel:${a.phone}" class="bg-red-600 hover:bg-red-500 text-white text-xs px-3 py-1.5 rounded flex items-center gap-1"><i class="fa-solid fa-phone"></i> Ara</a><button onclick="delSOS('${a.id}')" class="bg-slate-700 hover:bg-slate-600 text-white text-xs px-3 py-1.5 rounded">Çözüldü</button></div></div>`;
                });
            }
            servicesTable.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="5" class="text-center py-4 text-xs">Yükleniyor...</td></tr>';
            const { data: services } = await sb.from('services').select('*').order('created_at', {ascending: false});
            servicesTable.innerHTML = '';
            if(!services || services.length === 0) servicesTable.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="5" class="text-center py-4 text-xs">Kayıt yok.</td></tr>';
            else {
                services.forEach(s => {
                    let typeIcon = s.type === 'Tamirci' ? '<i class="fa-solid fa-wrench text-orange-400"></i>' : (s.type === 'Çekici' ? '<i class="fa-solid fa-truck-pickup text-yellow-400"></i>' : '<i class="fa-solid fa-building-flag text-red-400"></i>');
                    servicesTable.innerHTML += `<tr class="hover:bg-white/5 border-b border-slate-800 transition"><td class="px-4 py-3 font-bold text-white">${s.name}</td><td class="px-4 py-3 text-xs">${typeIcon} ${s.type}</td><td class="px-4 py-3"><span class="bg-slate-700 px-2 py-1 rounded text-[10px] text-white">${s.country}</span></td><td class="px-4 py-3 font-mono text-xs text-slate-300">${s.phone}</td><td class="px-4 py-3 text-right"><button onclick="delService('${s.id}')" class="text-red-400 hover:text-red-500 bg-red-500/10 p-1.5 rounded"><i class="fa-solid fa-trash"></i></button></td></tr>`;
                });
            }
        }
        async function delSOS(id) { if(confirm('Sorun çözüldü mü? Kayıt silinecek.')) { await sb.from('sos_alerts').delete().eq('id', id); loadSOS(); } }
        async function delService(id) { if(confirm('Hizmet silinsin mi?')) { await sb.from('services').delete().eq('id', id); loadSOS(); } }
        async function addService() {
            const { value: formValues } = await Swal.fire({ title: 'Yeni Hizmet Ekle', html: `<input id="swal-name" class="swal2-input" placeholder="Firma Adı"><select id="swal-type" class="swal2-input"><option value="Tamirci">Tamirci</option><option value="Çekici">Çekici</option><option value="Konsolosluk">Konsolosluk</option></select><input id="swal-country" class="swal2-input" placeholder="Ülke (Örn: Sırbistan)"><input id="swal-phone" class="swal2-input" placeholder="Telefon">`, focusConfirm: false, preConfirm: () => { return [ document.getElementById('swal-name').value, document.getElementById('swal-type').value, document.getElementById('swal-country').value, document.getElementById('swal-phone').value ] } });
            if (formValues) { const [name, type, country, phone] = formValues; if(!name || !phone) return; await sb.from('services').insert([{ name, type, country, phone, is_verified: true }]); loadSOS(); Swal.fire('Eklendi', '', 'success'); }
        }

        // --- WAZE (CANLI YOL BİLDİRİMLERİ) ---
        async function loadWaze() {
            const div = document.getElementById('wazeContainer');
            div.innerHTML = '<div class="col-span-4 text-center text-slate-500"><i class="fa-solid fa-spinner fa-spin text-2xl"></i><br>Bildirimler Yükleniyor...</div>';
            
            const { data, error } = await sb.from('road_reports').select('*').order('created_at', {ascending: false});
            if(error || !data) return;

            div.innerHTML = '';
            if(data.length === 0) div.innerHTML = '<div class="col-span-4 text-center text-slate-500">Henüz bildirim yok.</div>';

            data.forEach(r => {
                // Tip ikonları
                let icon = '<i class="fa-solid fa-circle-info"></i>';
                let color = 'border-slate-600';
                let textColor = 'text-slate-300';
                
                // MANTIKSAL EŞLEŞTİRME (SILA_YOLU.HTML İLE AYNI)
                if (r.report_type === 'Radar') { icon = '<i class="fa-solid fa-camera-retro"></i>'; color = 'border-blue-500'; textColor = 'text-blue-400'; }
                else if (r.report_type === 'Kaza') { icon = '<i class="fa-solid fa-car-burst"></i>'; color = 'border-red-500'; textColor = 'text-red-400'; }
                else if (r.report_type === 'Trafik') { icon = '<i class="fa-solid fa-car-side"></i>'; color = 'border-orange-500'; textColor = 'text-orange-400'; }
                else if (r.report_type === 'Calisma') { icon = '<i class="fa-solid fa-person-digging"></i>'; color = 'border-yellow-500'; textColor = 'text-yellow-400'; }
                else if (r.report_type === 'Polis') { icon = '<i class="fa-solid fa-user-police"></i>'; color = 'border-blue-800'; textColor = 'text-blue-500'; }
                else if (r.report_type === 'Mola') { icon = '<i class="fa-solid fa-mug-hot"></i>'; color = 'border-green-500'; textColor = 'text-green-400'; }

                // Harita Linki (Eğer koordinat varsa)
                let mapLink = '';
                if(r.lat && r.lng && r.lat !== 0) {
                    mapLink = `<a href="https://www.google.com/maps?q=${r.lat},${r.lng}" target="_blank" class="text-xs text-blue-400 hover:text-blue-300 flex items-center gap-1 mt-2"><i class="fa-solid fa-map-location-dot"></i> Konumu Gör</a>`;
                }

                div.innerHTML += `
                <div class="glass-panel p-5 rounded-2xl border ${color} bg-opacity-50 relative group">
                    <div class="flex justify-between items-start mb-3">
                        <div class="flex items-center gap-3">
                            <div class="w-10 h-10 rounded-full bg-slate-800 flex items-center justify-center text-xl ${textColor}">${icon}</div>
                            <div>
                                <h4 class="font-bold text-white text-sm">${r.report_type}</h4>
                                <span class="text-[10px] bg-slate-700 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-slate-300">${r.country_code || 'Avrupa'}</span>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                        <span class="text-[10px] text-slate-500">${new Date(r.created_at).toLocaleTimeString()}</span>
                    </div>
                    
                    <p class="text-sm text-slate-200 mb-2 line-clamp-2">"${r.description}"</p>
                    ${mapLink}
                    
                    <div class="flex justify-between items-center text-xs text-slate-400 border-t border-white/10 pt-3 mt-3">
                        <span class="flex items-center gap-1"><i class="fa-solid fa-user"></i> ${r.user_name || 'Anonim'}</span>
                        <span class="flex items-center gap-1 text-green-400 font-bold"><i class="fa-solid fa-thumbs-up"></i> ${r.confirmations || 0} Onay</span>
                    </div>

                    <button onclick="delReport('${r.id}')" class="absolute top-2 right-2 text-red-400 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition hover:bg-white/10 p-1.5 rounded"><i class="fa-solid fa-trash"></i></button>
                </div>`;
            });
        }

        async function delReport(id) { 
            if(confirm('Bu bildirim silinsin mi?')) { 
                await sb.from('road_reports').delete().eq('id', id); 
                loadWaze(); 
            } 
        }

    </script>
</body>
</html>
